!<mpls-te>

mpls traffic-eng

  cspf delay switch-over 60

  router-id 18.115.2.232
  reoptimize timers frequency 3600

  signalling graceful-restart

  signalling graceful-restart extend recovery-path

  signalling retransmit

  signalling refresh reduction

  signalling sd

  explicit-path name to-0.2WZHX2

    index 1 next-address strict 115.2.0.16
    index 2 next-address strict 115.2.0.11
  $

  explicit-path name exclude-0.2HX2

    index 1 exclude-address router-id 18.115.0.2
  $

  explicit-path name exculde-0.1HX1

    index 1 exclude-address router-id 18.115.0.1
